NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
S.T. SUNDARAM, A male child born to S. Thiyagarajan, on 27th May 1983, residing at No. 14-C, Keela Street,
Sindhupoondurai, Tirunelveli-627 001, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery
at Siva Vishnu Hospital, Bangaluru. The same has been medically examined by Dr. S. ANANDAKRISHNAKUMAR, M.D.D.P.M.,
Associate of Psychiatry, Tirunelveli Medical College. By this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be
known as S.T. OORMILA.
Tirunelveli,
4th June 2015.

S.T. SUNDARAM.

S. MARIAPPAN, A male child born to S. Senthurpandian on 17th May 1981, residing at No. 14-C, Keela Street,
Sindhupoondurai, Tirunelveli-627 001, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery at Siva
Vishnu Hospital, Bangaluru. The same has been medically examined by Dr. K. NEELATHATCHI, B.Sc., M.B.B.S., Medical
Officer, Govt. Primary Health Centre, Ukkirankottai, Tirunelveli, By this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be
known as S. KANNIGA.
Tirunelveli,
4th June 2015.

S. MARIAPPAN.

P. ARUMUGAM, A male child born to M. Palavesam on 21st May 1988, residing at No. 2/63, Perumal Koil Street,
Konda Nagaram, Tirunelveli-627 010, has been living as a female after an elaborate sexual reassignment surgery at
Siva Vishnu Hospital, Bangaluru. The same has been medically examined by Dr. K. NEELATHATCHI, B.Sc., M.B.B.S., Medical
Officer, Govt. Primary Health Centre, Ukkirankottai, Tirunelveli. By this I, may be treated as a female and shall henceforth be
known as P. ABINAYA.
Tirunelveli,
4th June 2015.

P. ARUMUGAM.
